\DoxyCodeLine{2708 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2709 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2710 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The operation completed successfully.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_OK                           S\_OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2715 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The device exists but is not currently attached.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_NOTATTACHED                  S\_FALSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2719 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The device buffer overflowed.  Some input was lost.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_BUFFEROVERFLOW               S\_FALSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The change in device properties had no effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_PROPNOEFFECT                 S\_FALSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2729 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The operation had no effect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_NOEFFECT                     S\_FALSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The device is a polled device.  As a result, device buffering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{ *  will not collect any data and event notifications will not be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{ *  signalled until GetDeviceState is called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_POLLEDDEVICE                 ((HRESULT)0x00000002L)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The parameters of the effect were successfully updated by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{comment}{ *  IDirectInputEffect::SetParameters, but the effect was not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{comment}{ *  downloaded because the device is not exclusively acquired}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{comment}{ *  or because the DIEP\_NODOWNLOAD flag was passed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DI\_DOWNLOADSKIPPED              ((HRESULT)0x00000003L)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
